# <a name="release-notes-for-semi-annual-channel-releases-in-2017"></a><span data-ttu-id="ffe95-103">在 2017年分號每年次通道版本的版本資訊</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ffe95-103">Release notes for Semi-Annual Channel releases in 2017</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="ffe95-104">這些版本資訊提供的新功能、 安全性更新及 2017年中包括分號每年次通道更新至 Office 365 ProPlus 中的非安全性更新的相關資訊。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ffe95-104">These release notes provide information about new features, security updates, and non-security updates that are included in Semi-Annual Channel updates to Office 365 ProPlus in 2017.</span></span> 
> [!NOTE]
> - <span data-ttu-id="ffe95-105">下列也提供資訊的新功能、 安全性更新及非安全性更新 Visio Pro for Office 365 及 Project Online 桌面用戶端。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ffe95-105">The following also provides information about new features, security updates, and non-security updates for Visio Pro for Office 365 and Project Online Desktop Client.</span></span>
> - <span data-ttu-id="ffe95-106">此資訊也適用於 Office 365 商務是隨附 Office 365 計劃，例如企業進階版的 Office 版本。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ffe95-106">This information also applies to Office 365 Business, which is the version of Office that comes with some Office 365 plans, such as Business Premium.</span></span>
> - <span data-ttu-id="ffe95-107">分號每年次通道命名為已延期通道年 1 月 2018年之前。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ffe95-107">Semi-Annual Channel was named Deferred Channel prior to January 2018.</span></span>

### <a name="access-feature-updates"></a><span data-ttu-id="ffe95-172">Access： 功能更新</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ffe95-172">Access: Feature updates</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="ffe95-173">**什麼是 [新增] 對話方塊：** 會醒目提示新的 Access 功能對話方塊隨即顯示 Access 開啟後存取更新新功能時。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ffe95-173">**What’s New dialog:** A dialog box that highlights new Access features appears when Access is opened after Access is updated with new features.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ffe95-174">[] 對話方塊是也移至檔案\>帳戶\>的新功能。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ffe95-174">The dialog box is also available by going to File \> Account \> What’s New.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="ffe95-175">**大量 (bigint) 支援：** 使用大量資料型別 Access 資料表中計算大的數字，以及連結到或匯入來自使用對等的資料類型，例如 bigint SQL Server 中的外部資料庫。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ffe95-175">**Large Number (bigint) support:** Use the Large Number data type in Access tables to calculate large numbers, and to link to or import from external databases that use an equivalent data type, such as bigint in SQL Server.</span></span> [<span data-ttu-id="ffe95-176">更多資訊</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ffe95-176">More information</span></span>](https://blogs.office.com/2017/03/06/new-in-access-2016-large-number-bigint-support/)

### <a name="excel-feature-updates"></a><span data-ttu-id="ffe95-177">Excel： 功能更新</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ffe95-177">Excel: Feature updates</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="ffe95-178">**Windows 資訊保護 (WIP) 支援：**  Excel 現在是開明應用程式，且能區分公司和個人資料，正確地判斷要 protect、 根據設定的原則。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ffe95-178">**Windows Information Protection (WIP) support:**   Excel is now an enlightened app, and can differentiate between corporate and personal data, correctly determining which to protect, based on configured policies.</span></span>  [<span data-ttu-id="ffe95-179">更多資訊</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ffe95-179">More information</span></span>](https://aka.ms/wiptechnet)
-   <span data-ttu-id="ffe95-180">**取得 & 轉換改進：** 在查詢編輯器中，以提供範例值建立新的欄。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ffe95-180">**Get & Transform improvement:** In the Query Editor, create a new column by providing sample values.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ffe95-181">當您輸入時，Excel 會偵測所需的轉換及顯示新欄的預覽。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ffe95-181">As you type, Excel detects the required transformations and shows a preview of the new column.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="ffe95-182">**插入最近的連結：** 輕鬆地附加至最近使用的雲端架構檔案或網站的超連結並建立使用螢幕助讀程式的人員的有意義的顯示名稱。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ffe95-182">**Insert recent links:** Easily attach hyperlinks to recent cloud-based files or websites, and create meaningful display names for people using screen readers.</span></span> [<span data-ttu-id="ffe95-183">更多資訊</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ffe95-183">More information</span></span>](https://support.office.com/article/002684c4-bf06-422b-821f-b4ef84fdb0e3)
-   <span data-ttu-id="ffe95-184">**個人化的預設樞紐分析表版面配置：** 設定樞紐分析表，以及每次您建立新的樞紐分析表的開頭的版面配置的方式。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ffe95-184">**Personalize the default PivotTable layout:** Set up a PivotTable the way you like, and start with that layout every time you create a new PivotTable.</span></span> [<span data-ttu-id="ffe95-185">更多資訊</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ffe95-185">More information</span></span>](https://support.office.com/article/efd8569c-f07a-43c1-9db2-4f2912a0f94e)
-   <span data-ttu-id="ffe95-186">**取得 & 轉換為增強功能：** 使用者可以範例建立新的欄和列配置分割表格欄。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ffe95-186">**Get & Transform improvements:** Users can create new columns by example and split table columns into rows.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ffe95-187">指定用以 SAP HANA 參數與群組資料現在會比較容易。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ffe95-187">Specifying parameters to SAP HANA and grouping data is now easier.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="ffe95-188">**集中式部署的增益集**： 系統管理員可以部署和 Office 365 系統管理中心增益集更新為使用者或群組。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ffe95-188">**Centralized deployment of add-ins**: Admins can deploy and update add-ins to users or groups from the Office 365 admin center.</span></span> [<span data-ttu-id="ffe95-189">更多資訊</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ffe95-189">More information</span></span>](https://dev.office.com/docs/add-ins/publish/centralized-deployment)
-   <span data-ttu-id="ffe95-190">**快速存取工具列自訂：** 下標和上標圖示可以新增至快速存取工具列。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ffe95-190">**Quick Access Toolbar customization:** The Subscript and Superscript icons can be added to the Quick Access Toolbar.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="ffe95-191">**取得 & 轉換為增強功能：** 自動偵測的分隔符號字元分割資料行使用查詢編輯器中，選擇要合併二進位檔搭配使用的範例檔案並指定套件集合時使用 DB2 連接器連線時。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ffe95-191">**Get & Transform improvements:** Automatic detection of delimiter character when splitting columns using the Query Editor, choose which sample file to use with Combine Binaries, and specify the package collection to connect to when using the DB2 Connector.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="ffe95-192">**阿布達比字型：** 支援西歐語言以及使用阿拉伯指令碼的主要語言的字型系列。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ffe95-192">**Dubai font:** Font family that supports both Western European languages as well as the major languages that use the Arabic script.</span></span> [<span data-ttu-id="ffe95-193">更多資訊</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ffe95-193">More information</span></span>](https://support.office.com/article/c862df16-ae0d-46d9-b117-aa3f41f9706e)
-   <span data-ttu-id="ffe95-194">**背景移除：** 移除的自由格式的繪圖工具的圖片背景。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ffe95-194">**Background removal:** Remove a picture background with a free-form drawing tool.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="ffe95-195">**取得 & 轉換為增強功能：**「 選取相關資料表 」 在 [導覽] 對話方塊以使用 ODCB 和 OLEDB 連接器、 結合多個檔案直接從資料夾資料預覽] 對話方塊中，並使用新的快顯功能表選項 [查詢編輯器] 視窗中現有的查詢中插入新的步驟。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ffe95-195">**Get & Transform improvements:** Use “Select Related Tables” in the Navigator dialog with the ODCB and OLEDB connectors, combine multiple files directly from the folder Data Preview dialog, and use a new context menu option in the Query Editor window to insert new steps in existing queries.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="ffe95-196">**用於選取及變更物件的畫筆：** 取得物件控點以調整大小、 旋轉、 移動、 數位畫筆等等。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ffe95-196">**Use a pen to select and change objects:** Grab object handles with a digital pen to resize, rotate, move, and more.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="ffe95-197">**對應圖表：** 比較的值並顯示不同地理區域的類別。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ffe95-197">**Map Chart:** Compare values and show categories across geographic regions.</span></span> [<span data-ttu-id="ffe95-198">更多資訊</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ffe95-198">More information</span></span>](https://support.office.com/article/f2cfed55-d622-42cd-8ec9-ec8a358b593b)
-   <span data-ttu-id="ffe95-199">**SVG 圖像：** 插入及編輯活頁簿中的可調整的向量圖形 (SVG)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ffe95-199">**SVG images:** Insert and edit scalable vector graphics (SVG) in workbooks.</span></span> [<span data-ttu-id="ffe95-200">更多資訊</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ffe95-200">More information</span></span>](https://support.office.com/article/69f29d39-194a-4072-8c35-dbe5e7ea528c)
-   <span data-ttu-id="ffe95-201">**插入圖示：** 使用標準文件庫的可擴充的向量圖形 (SVG) 檔案移至插入圖示\>圖例\>圖示。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ffe95-201">**Insert icons:**  Use icons from a standard library of scalable vector graphics (SVG) files by going to Insert \> Illustrations \> Icons.</span></span> [<span data-ttu-id="ffe95-202">更多資訊</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ffe95-202">More information</span></span>](https://support.office.com/article/e2459f17-3996-4795-996e-b9a13486fa79)
-   <span data-ttu-id="ffe95-203">**儲存至最新的資料夾：** 使用 [最近] 索引標籤當您移至 [檔案儲存至最近使用過資料夾的活頁簿\>另存新檔。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ffe95-203">**Save to Recent folders:** Save a workbook to a recently used folder by using the Recent tab when you go to File \> Save As.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="ffe95-204">**協助工具功能改良：** 使用鍵盤、 [朗讀程式] 和其他輔助技術，閱讀並編輯活頁簿的改良的支援。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ffe95-204">**Accessibility improvements:** Improved support for using the keyboard, Narrator, and other assistive technology to read and edit workbooks.</span></span> [<span data-ttu-id="ffe95-205">更多資訊</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ffe95-205">More information</span></span>](https://support.office.com/article/51fcb17a-b15b-4b13-ae04-d4f38ece3f78)

### <a name="excel-non-security-updates"></a><span data-ttu-id="ffe95-212">Excel： 的非安全性更新</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ffe95-212">Excel: Non-security updates</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="ffe95-213">修正與複製並貼到 Excel、 忽略 tab 字元分隔的 HTML 文字、 不正確地移除空白列及欄、 忽略對齊、 及忽略公式等問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ffe95-213">Fix issues with copying and pasting into Excel, such as ignoring tab-separated HTML text, incorrectly removing empty rows and columns, ignoring alignment, and ignoring formulas.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="ffe95-214">修正問題時嘗試將變更儲存至文件進行同步處理 OneDrive 用戶端錯誤出現的位置。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ffe95-214">Fix an issue where errors appear when trying to save changes to documents synchronized with the OneDrive client.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="ffe95-215">修正問題其中 Excel 在將工作表資料新增至資料模型時，且高對比佈景主題設定為黑色。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ffe95-215">Fix an issue where Excel crashes when adding worksheet data to a Data Model and the High Contrast theme is set to Black.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="ffe95-216">修正問題 Excel 活頁簿包含外部連結的損毀的位置。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ffe95-216">Fix an issue where Excel crashes for workbooks that contain external links.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="ffe95-217">修正問題其中貼上從 Excel 至字的儲存格顯示儲存格中零時即使未選取"零中有零值的儲存格的 Show"的設定。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ffe95-217">Fix an issue where pasting cells from Excel to Word shows zeros in the cells, even though the "Show a zero in cells that have zero value" setting is not selected.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="ffe95-218">修正問題 Excel 不會將設定套用以程式設計方式建立 Excel 2010 中或更早版本的活頁簿時的工作表保護密碼。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ffe95-218">Fix an issue where Excel doesn't set the sheet protection password when applied programmatically for workbooks created in Excel 2010 or earlier.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="ffe95-219">修正問題其中合併為中心未作用群組工作表中。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ffe95-219">Fix an issue where Merge & Center doesn't work in grouped worksheets.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="ffe95-220">修正問題其中已導入後版本的 Office 2016-例如的新功能、 TEXTJOIN、 CONCAT、 IFS、 MAXIFS、 和 MINIFS-均遺失。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ffe95-220">Fix an issue where new functions that were introduced after the release of Office 2016 - for example, TEXTJOIN, CONCAT, IFS, MAXIFS, and MINIFS - are missing.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="ffe95-221">當使用者嘗試將儲存格層級權限套用 Excel 當機修正問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ffe95-221">Fix an issue where Excel crashes when the user attempts to apply cell level permissions.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="ffe95-222">修正問題其中將大型檔案儲存至 OneDrive for Business 會導致鎖定檔案，且使用者無法編輯檔案直到使用者關閉並重新開啟 Excel。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ffe95-222">Fix an issue where saving a large file to OneDrive for Business causes the file to be locked and the user can't edit the file until the user closes and reopens Excel.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="ffe95-223">在新視窗出現的位置灰色.xls 活頁簿開啟時修正問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ffe95-223">Fix an issue where a new window appears grayed out when an .xls workbook is opened.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="ffe95-224">修正問題其中 Excel 可能會損毀插入超連結。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ffe95-224">Fix an issue where Excel might crash when inserting hyperlinks.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="ffe95-225">修正問題其中 Excel 可能會失敗時新增 XML 對應。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ffe95-225">Fix an issue where Excel might fail when adding XML Maps.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="ffe95-226">其中命令按鈕的增益集未作用中之增益集，以便在升級之後或移除和一次下載增益集來自 Office 市集後修正問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ffe95-226">Fix an issue where the command button for an Add-in doesn't work after the add-in is upgraded or after removing and downloading the Add-in again from the Office store.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="ffe95-227">修正問題其中 Excel 可能會損毀操作透過 VBA 的 DLL 工作表。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ffe95-227">Fix an issue where Excel might crash when manipulating DLL sheets via VBA.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="ffe95-228">選取圖表上的表單控制項下拉式方塊時 Excel 當機修正問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ffe95-228">Fix an issue where Excel crashes when selecting a form control combo box on a chart sheet.</span></span>

### <a name="outlook-feature-updates"></a><span data-ttu-id="ffe95-235">Outlook： 功能更新</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ffe95-235">Outlook: Feature updates</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="ffe95-236">**Windows 資訊保護 (WIP) 支援：**  Outlook 現在是開明應用程式，且能區分公司和個人資料，正確地判斷要 protect、 根據設定的原則。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ffe95-236">**Windows Information Protection (WIP) support:**   Outlook is now an enlightened app, and can differentiate between corporate and personal data, correctly determining which to protect, based on configured policies.</span></span>  [<span data-ttu-id="ffe95-237">更多資訊</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ffe95-237">More information</span></span>](https://aka.ms/wiptechnet)
-   <span data-ttu-id="ffe95-238">**插入最近的連結：** 附加至最近使用的雲端架構檔案或網站的超連結，並建立使用螢幕助讀程式的人員的有意義的顯示名稱。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ffe95-238">**Insert recent links:** Attach hyperlinks to recent cloud-based files or websites, and create meaningful display names for people using screen readers.</span></span> [<span data-ttu-id="ffe95-239">更多資訊</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ffe95-239">More information</span></span>](https://support.office.com/article/002684c4-bf06-422b-821f-b4ef84fdb0e3)
-   <span data-ttu-id="ffe95-240">**阿布達比字型：** 支援西歐語言以及使用阿拉伯指令碼的主要語言的字型系列。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ffe95-240">**Dubai font:** Font family that supports both Western European languages as well as the major languages that use the Arabic script.</span></span> [<span data-ttu-id="ffe95-241">更多資訊</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ffe95-241">More information</span></span>](https://support.office.com/article/c862df16-ae0d-46d9-b117-aa3f41f9706e)
-   <span data-ttu-id="ffe95-242">**背景移除：** 移除的自由格式的繪圖工具的圖片背景。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ffe95-242">**Background removal:** Remove a picture background with a free-form drawing tool.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="ffe95-243">**檢查存取共用檔案：** Outlook 告訴使用者隨時若收件者可能無法存取附加的 OneDrive 或 SharePoint 檔案，並且建議如何修正問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ffe95-243">**Check access to shared files:** Outlook tells the user ahead of time if recipients may not be able to access an attached OneDrive or SharePoint file, and suggests how to fix the issue.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="ffe95-244">**設定的權限的附件：** Onedrive for SharePoint 附件的使用者可以設定收件者組織或外部，擁有讀取或編輯附件的權限。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ffe95-244">**Set permissions on attachments:** For OneDrive or SharePoint attachments, the user can set whether recipients, in the organization or externally, have read or edit permissions to the attachment.</span></span>

-   <span data-ttu-id="ffe95-247">**SVG 圖像：** 插入及編輯電子郵件中的可調整的向量圖形 (SVG)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ffe95-247">**SVG images:** Insert and edit scalable vector graphics (SVG) in emails.</span></span> [<span data-ttu-id="ffe95-248">更多資訊</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ffe95-248">More information</span></span>](https://support.office.com/article/69f29d39-194a-4072-8c35-dbe5e7ea528c)
-   <span data-ttu-id="ffe95-249">**插入圖示：** 使用標準文件庫的可擴充的向量圖形 (SVG) 檔案移至插入圖示\>圖例\>圖示。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ffe95-249">**Insert icons:**  Use icons from a standard library of scalable vector graphics (SVG) files by going to Insert \> Illustrations \> Icons.</span></span>  [<span data-ttu-id="ffe95-250">更多資訊</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ffe95-250">More information</span></span>](https://support.office.com/article/e2459f17-3996-4795-996e-b9a13486fa79)

### <a name="skype-for-business-feature-updates"></a><span data-ttu-id="ffe95-336">Skype for Business： 更新的功能</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ffe95-336">Skype for Business: Feature updates</span></span>

-   <span data-ttu-id="ffe95-340">**Windows 資訊保護 (WIP) 支援：** 適用於企業的 Skype 現在已經支援為 WIP 工時僅應用程式。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ffe95-340">**Windows Information Protection (WIP) support:** Skype for Business is now supported as a WIP-work only app.</span></span>  <span data-ttu-id="ffe95-341">允許應用程式清單中新增 Skype，它會指出 Windows 它不會處理個人資料。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ffe95-341">By adding Skype to your allowed apps list, it indicates to Windows that it does not handle personal data.</span></span>  <span data-ttu-id="ffe95-342">Windows 會保護資料安全性代表 Skype for Business。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ffe95-342">Windows will protect data on behalf of Skype for Business.</span></span>  [<span data-ttu-id="ffe95-343">更多資訊</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ffe95-343">More information</span></span>](https://aka.ms/wiptechnet)

### <a name="excel-feature-updates"></a><span data-ttu-id="ffe95-496">Excel： 功能更新</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ffe95-496">Excel: Feature updates</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="ffe95-497">**資料轉換] 和 [連線增強功能：** 展開清單將新文字欄與值之間的分隔字元並連線至 SQL 時指定容錯移轉] 選項。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ffe95-497">**Data transformation and connectivity enhancements:** Expand a list into a new text column with delimiter between the values, and specify a failover option when connecting to SQL.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="ffe95-498">**資料轉換] 和 [連線增強功能：** 現在已經支援百分比資料類型、 與二進位結合函數製作體驗目前已經強化功能。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ffe95-498">**Data transformation and connectivity enhancements:** The Percentage data type is now supported, and binary combining function authoring experiences have been enhanced.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="ffe95-499">**OLEDB 連接器：** 使用 OLEDB 連接器 Get 轉換中的建立資料匯入藉由指定連接字串以及選用的 SQL 陳述式來執行查詢。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ffe95-499">**OLEDB connector:** Use the OLEDB connector in Get & Transform to create a query to import data by specifying a Connection String and, optionally, a SQL statement to execute.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="ffe95-500">**筆跡重新顯示：** 移至 [繪製\>筆跡重新顯示重新顯示手寫正向和回溯隱藏及顯示的內容，提供逐步指示，或更容易理解的其他人的想法流程。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ffe95-500">**Ink replay:** Go to Draw \> Ink Replay to replay handwriting forward and backward to hide and reveal content, provide step-by-step instructions, or better understand the flow of others’ thoughts.</span></span> [<span data-ttu-id="ffe95-501">更多資訊</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ffe95-501">More information</span></span>](https://support.office.com/article/fa4f044f-810b-43fe-b774-da04a0b37496)
-   <span data-ttu-id="ffe95-502">**CSV (utf-8) 支援：** 開啟並使用 utf-8 字元編碼的 CSV 檔案的儲存位置。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ffe95-502">**CSV (UTF-8) support:** Open and save CSV files that use UTF-8 character encoding.</span></span>

-   <span data-ttu-id="ffe95-630">[CVE-2017年-8550](https://portal.msrc.microsoft.com/en-us/security-guidance/advisory/CVE-2017-8550)： 適用於商務遠端程式碼執行弱點 Skype</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ffe95-630">[CVE-2017-8550](https://portal.msrc.microsoft.com/en-us/security-guidance/advisory/CVE-2017-8550): Skype for Business Remote Code Execution Vulnerability</span></span>

### <a name="skype-for-business-non-security-updates"></a><span data-ttu-id="ffe95-631">Skype for Business： 的非安全性更新</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ffe95-631">Skype for Business: Non-security updates</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="ffe95-632">修正問題導致開啟為標準的視窗，而不是自動接受交談的交談] 視窗最小化狀態，並預期地從其他 windows 取得焦點。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ffe95-632">Fix an issue that causes a conversation window for an automatically accepted conversation to open as a normal window, instead of minimized, and unexpectedly take focus away from other windows.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="ffe95-633">修正使用者是無法登入內部和外部的公司網路之間切換時所發生問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ffe95-633">Fix an issue where users are unable to sign in when switching between inside and outside corporate networks.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="ffe95-634">變更用來允許或拒絕參與者的文字 （X 或核取記號表示） 的圖像大廳按鈕。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ffe95-634">Change the lobby buttons used to admit or deny participants from text to images (an X or a checkmark).</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="ffe95-635">變更會議提醒通知文字從"接受""加入"。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ffe95-635">Change the meeting reminder notification text from "Accept" to "Join."</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="ffe95-636">更新的 IM 寄件者收件者的狀態設為 [請勿打擾] 時顯示訊息。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ffe95-636">Update the message shown to the sender of an IM when the recipient's status is set to Do Not Disturb.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="ffe95-637">更新時收件者已離線和"儲存歷程記錄 」 已停用，使其清除的 IM、 寄件者顯示的訊息收件者將不會收到訊息。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ffe95-637">Update the message shown to the sender of an IM, when the recipient is offline and "saving to history" is disabled, to make it clear that the recipient won't receive the message.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="ffe95-638">新增聊天歷程記錄和名冊中群組聊天之間移動垂直分割軸的功能。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ffe95-638">Add the capability to move the vertical splitter bar between the chat history and the roster in a group chat.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="ffe95-639">新增調整大小的 IM] 或 [聊天室] 視窗中的索引標籤清單的功能。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ffe95-639">Add the capability to resize the list of tabs in IM or chat room windows.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="ffe95-640">新增選取搜尋建立主題摘要時的聊天室的功能。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ffe95-640">Add the capability to select the chat rooms searched when creating a topic feed.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="ffe95-641">修正問題訊息停止出現的聊天歷程記錄大西洋交談。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ffe95-641">Fix an issue where message stop appearing in chat history mid-conversation.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="ffe95-642">修正問題重複的訊息出現在 [交談] 視窗中的位置。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ffe95-642">Fix an issue where duplicate messages appear in the conversation window.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="ffe95-643">修正其中吐司通知動作 （接受並略過） 未正確顯示通知大量期間發生問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ffe95-643">Fix an issue where toast notification actions (Accept and Ignore) aren't properly displayed during a high volume of notifications.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="ffe95-644">修正問題，使用者無法輸入其中一則訊息之後使用 Alt + tab 鍵來開啟 [最小化的交談] 視窗。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ffe95-644">Fix an issue where the user can't type a message after using Alt+Tab to open a minimized conversation window.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="ffe95-645">修正問題 IM] 按鈕會變為灰色出在使用者的連絡人卡片即使 IM 為可用。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ffe95-645">Fix an issue where the IM button is grayed out in the contact card for a user, even though IM is available.</span></span>

-   <span data-ttu-id="ffe95-647">修正問題其中自訂連結不時選取 [啟動]。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ffe95-647">Fix an issue where custom links don't launch when selected.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="ffe95-648">修正問題其中 [區域] 欄位中的線上會議文字不正確顯示非英文字元。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ffe95-648">Fix an issue where the online meeting text in the Region field isn't displayed correctly for non-English characters.</span></span>

-   <span data-ttu-id="ffe95-650">修正的問題，建立主題摘要時, 清除搜尋結果不會重設結果為已瀏覽過的會議室清單。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ffe95-650">Fix an issue where, when creating a topic feed, clearing the search results doesn't reset the results to a list of followed rooms.</span></span>

-   <span data-ttu-id="ffe95-653">修正問題其中預設焦點時，無法在聊天室輸入] 區域中的公式會停用的分頁的交談。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ffe95-653">Fix an issue where the default focus isn't in the chat input area when tabbed conversations are disabled.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="ffe95-654">修正問題其中"忘記您的電話撥入 PIN 嗎？ 」</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ffe95-654">Fix an issue where the "Forgot your dial-in PIN?"</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ffe95-655">連結不會出現在會議邀請。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ffe95-655">link doesn't appear in the meeting invite.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="ffe95-656">在 [一般] 和 [音訊裝置頁面上修正的問題其中一些文字是裁剪，將會遭到截斷時使用高 DPI 螢幕顯示 175%或更高。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ffe95-656">Fix an issue where some text is clipped and truncated on the General and Audio device pages when using high DPI screens at 175% display or higher.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="ffe95-657">修正問題時電腦已暫停或繼續時沒有網路和電腦是"一律在、 永遠連線 (AOAC") 的電腦上的商務 Skype 損毀。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ffe95-657">Fix an issue where Skype for Business crashes when the computer is suspended or resumed when there is no network and the computer is an "always on, always connected (AOAC)" computer.</span></span>

-   <span data-ttu-id="ffe95-659">修正問題其中例如選擇連結\\ \\servername 或 file:// IM 訊息中的會產生錯誤訊息而不是開啟該位置。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ffe95-659">Fix an issue where choosing a link such as \\\\servername or file:// in an IM message results in an error message instead of opening the location.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="ffe95-660">使用以位置為主路由，使用者無法進行或收到 PSTN 通話是因為伺服器會認為使用者的位置不是有效的 PSTN 通話其中虛擬桌面基礎結構 (VDI) 環境中修正問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ffe95-660">Fix an issue, in a Virtual Desktop Infrastructure (VDI) environment that uses location-based routing, where the user can't make or receive PSTN calls because the server thinks the location of the user isn't valid for PSTN calls.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="ffe95-661">變更使用者的狀態設為 [請勿打擾] 或簡報、 從時未接的郵件傳送的電子郵件的主旨行"未接的交談\<名稱\>"到"\<名稱\>傳送 Skype for Business 中的郵件。 」</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ffe95-661">Change the subject line of the email sent for a missed message, when the user's status is set to Do Not Disturb or Presenting, from "Missed conversation with \<name\>" to "\<Name\> sent you a message in Skype for Business."</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="ffe95-662">啟動擷取第一次登入裝置上的時間戳記[普查資料](https://docs.microsoft.com/skypeforbusiness/legal-and-regulatory/data-collection-practices)來協助識別登入可靠性趨勢的一部分。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ffe95-662">Start capturing the timestamp for the first time sign-in on the device as part of [census data](https://docs.microsoft.com/skypeforbusiness/legal-and-regulatory/data-collection-practices) to help identify sign-in reliability trends.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="ffe95-663">修正問題不某些監視器上具備設定視窗 10 版本 1607 (也稱為紀念日 Update) 會顯示共用次要監視器選項。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ffe95-663">Fix an issue where the option to share a secondary monitor doesn't appear with certain monitor configurations on Window 10 Version 1607 (also known as the Anniversary Update).</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="ffe95-664">其中 Skype 商務當機次數時共享者會使用第 3 時將顯示比例都會共用內容的協力廠商的 RDP 實作修正問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ffe95-664">Fix an issue where Skype for Business crashes when zooming into shared content when the sharer is using a 3rd party implementation of RDP.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="ffe95-665">修正問題當使用者按一下 [音訊通話虛擬桌面基礎結構 (VDI) 環境中的 [控制項] 按鈕上時不會出現的音訊控制台中的位置。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ffe95-665">Fix an issue where the Audio Controls panel doesn't appear when a user clicks on the controls button in an audio call in a Virtual Desktop Infrastructure (VDI) environment.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="ffe95-666">修正問題時使用者正在執行 Windows 7 和先、 共用的主要監視器，然後再切換共用第二個監視器的檢視器看到螢幕變黑的位置。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ffe95-666">Fix an issue where viewers see a black screen when a user is running Windows 7 and shares the main monitor first, and then switches to share a second monitor.</span></span>

-   <span data-ttu-id="ffe95-675">修正問題時登入後繼續 for Business Skype 停止回應。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ffe95-675">Fix an issue where Skype for Business hangs when signing in after resuming.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="ffe95-676">會議連結已停用如果在這兩個組織的 Exchange 伺服器已停用 TNEF 修正問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ffe95-676">Fix an issue where the meeting link is disabled if the Exchange servers in both organizations have TNEF disabled.</span></span>

-   <span data-ttu-id="ffe95-678">白板上的文字註釋出都會遺失時為 PNG 檔案儲存在白板修正問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ffe95-678">Fix an issue where text annotations on a whiteboard are lost when saving the whiteboard as an PNG file.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="ffe95-679">修正問題時輸入超過並列文字日文 IM 視窗中的第一行隱藏的位置。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ffe95-679">Fix an issue where the first line is hidden when inputting over two lines in Japanese in the IM window.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="ffe95-680">修正問題其中 & 字元 (&) 不正確地以此名稱中有底線。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ffe95-680">Fix an issue where the ampersand character (&) is incorrectly replaced by an underscore character in names.</span></span>

-   <span data-ttu-id="ffe95-682">修正問題其中滑鼠停留在視窗不會啟動視窗即使作業系統設定若要這樣做。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ffe95-682">Fix an issue where hovering the mouse over a window doesn't activate the window even though the operating system is configured to do that.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="ffe95-683">修正問題其中傳出電話交談歷程記錄項目顯示來電者，而不是呼叫方。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ffe95-683">Fix an issue where outgoing call conversation history items shows the caller instead of the called party.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="ffe95-684">修正問題之 F12 不會在本機上儲存交談。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ffe95-684">Fix an issue where the F12 doesn't locally save a conversation.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="ffe95-685">其中的未接的交談電子郵件不包含初始 IM 修正問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ffe95-685">Fix an issue where a missed conversation email doesn't contain the initial IM.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="ffe95-686">其中 emoji 可以新增 IM 文字區域即使簡報者已停用 IM 參與修正問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ffe95-686">Fix an issue where an emoji can be added in the IM text area even if the presenter has disabled IM participation.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="ffe95-687">使用 [鈴聲與音效] 選項] 對話方塊上的版面配置修正問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ffe95-687">Fix an issue with the layout of the Ringtones and Sounds option dialog box.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="ffe95-688">修正問題時關閉 [交談] 視窗的商務 Skype 損毀。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ffe95-688">Fix an issue where Skype for Business crashes when closing a conversation window.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="ffe95-689">修正問題時網域註冊為虛名網域的 DNS 較不登入失敗時。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ffe95-689">Fix an issue where DNS-less sign in fails when the domain is registered as a vanity domain.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="ffe95-690">修正問題常設聊天室通知設定其不進行另存成或載入正確。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ffe95-690">Fix an issue where persistent chat notification settings aren't being saved or loaded correctly.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="ffe95-691">修正其中現有的對等交談視窗或聊天室不顯示即使並重新開啟交談設定登入之後發生問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ffe95-691">Fix an issue where existing peer-to-peer conversation windows or chat rooms aren't showing up after signing in even though the setting to reopen conversations is set.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="ffe95-692">修正問題靜音或解除靜音作用中的交談會使其他交談視窗中看起來像擁有未讀取的郵件。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ffe95-692">Fix an issue where muting or unmuting the active conversation causes other conversation windows to appear as if they have unread messages.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="ffe95-693">修正設定媒體旁路的使用者是無法繼續來自 PSTN 閘道的通話他們將該來電放入保留之後所發生問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ffe95-693">Fix an issue where users that are configured for media bypass are unable to resume a call from a PSTN gateway after they put that call on hold.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="ffe95-694">其中使用者會看到藍色方塊，而不是影片透過加入會議時更新 URL 時使用的第 3 協力廠商的 RDP 實作修正問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ffe95-694">Fix an issue where the user sees a blue box instead of the video when joining a meeting via a URL when using a 3rd party implementation of RDP.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="ffe95-695">修正問題的 SIP 位址的使用者部分，而不吐司警示中的顯示名稱的顯示位置。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ffe95-695">Fix an issue where the user part of the SIP address is showing instead of the display name in a toast alert.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="ffe95-696">修正的問題，當 Skype for Business 連線至 SIP 伺服器連接埠 443 上與 proxy 伺服器 is present、 有大幅延遲登入程序中如果 proxy 不允許這類連線。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ffe95-696">Fix an issue where, when Skype for Business connects to a SIP server over port 443 and a proxy server is present, there is a significant delay in the sign-in process if the proxy doesn't allow such connections.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ffe95-697">修正啟用新增下 HKEY EnableDetectProxyForAllConnections DWORD 登錄項目\_目前\_使用者\\軟體\\Microsoft\\UCCPlatform\\Lync，並將值設定為 1。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ffe95-697">The fix is enabled by adding the EnableDetectProxyForAllConnections DWORD registry entry under HKEY\_CURRENT\_USER\\Software\\Microsoft\\UCCPlatform\\Lync, and setting the value to 1.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="ffe95-698">其中時使用的分頁的交談，按兩下 [] 索引標籤上，並啟動輸入有時會導致將焦點移至不同的索引標籤，並繼續在該交談] 視窗中輸入修正問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ffe95-698">Fix an issue where, when using tabbed conversations, double-clicking on a tab and starting to type can sometimes cause the focus to move to a different tab and continue the typing in that conversation window.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="ffe95-699">其中 Url 立即訊息中包含無法選取 [聊天歷程記錄] 視窗中使用鍵盤修正問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ffe95-699">Fix an issue where URLs included in an instant message can't be selected in the chat history window by using the keyboard.</span></span>

### <a name="skype-for-business-non-security-updates"></a><span data-ttu-id="ffe95-951">Skype for Business： 的非安全性更新</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ffe95-951">Skype for Business: Non-security updates</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="ffe95-952">修正問題不某些監視器上具備設定視窗 10 版本 1607 (也稱為紀念日 Update) 會顯示共用次要監視器選項。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ffe95-952">Fix an issue where the option to share a secondary monitor doesn't appear with certain monitor configurations on Window 10 Version 1607 (also known as the Anniversary Update).</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="ffe95-953">其中 Skype 商務當機次數時共享者會使用第 3 時將顯示比例都會共用內容的協力廠商的 RDP 實作修正問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ffe95-953">Fix an issue where Skype for Business crashes when zooming into shared content when the sharer is using a 3rd party implementation of RDP.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="ffe95-954">修正的問題，當 Skype for Business 連線至 SIP 伺服器連接埠 443 上與 proxy 伺服器 is present、 有大幅延遲登入程序中如果 proxy 不允許這類連線。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ffe95-954">Fix an issue where, when Skype for Business connects to a SIP server over port 443 and a proxy server is present, there is a significant delay in the sign-in process if the proxy doesn't allow such connections.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="ffe95-955">修正啟用新增下 HKEY EnableDetectProxyForAllConnections DWORD 登錄項目\_目前\_使用者\\軟體\\Microsoft\\UCCPlatform\\Lync，並將值設定為 1。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ffe95-955">The fix is enabled by adding the EnableDetectProxyForAllConnections DWORD registry entry under HKEY\_CURRENT\_USER\\Software\\Microsoft\\UCCPlatform\\Lync, and setting the value to 1.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="ffe95-956">修正問題時使用者正在執行 Windows 7 和先、 共用的主要監視器，然後再切換共用第二個監視器的檢視器看到螢幕變黑的位置。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ffe95-956">Fix an issue where viewers see a black screen when a user is running Windows 7 and shares the main monitor first, and then switches to share a second monitor.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="ffe95-957">修正問題其中使用者無法連線至 Exchange 使用者已移轉至 Exchange Online 後取得交談記錄、 連絡人或語音信箱資訊。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ffe95-957">Fix an issue where the user can't connect to Exchange to get conversation history, contact, or voicemail information after the user has been migrated to Exchange Online.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="ffe95-958">修正問題與其中嘗試不正確地將資訊貼到撥號鍵台或白板中的文字註貼到資訊 [交談] 輸入的文字方塊中的 [交談] 視窗。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ffe95-958">Fix an issue with the conversation window where trying to paste information into the dial pad or into text annotations in the whiteboard incorrectly pastes the information into the chat input text box.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="ffe95-959">修正問題 for Business Skype 不更新時使用不同的解決方法，特別是高解析度的監視器監視器與監視變更縮放比例。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ffe95-959">Fix an issue where Skype for Business doesn't update scaling with monitor changes when using monitors with different resolutions, especially high resolution monitors.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="ffe95-960">修正的問題時若要檢視清單中的 IM 轉換中的參與者使用鍵盤，, 鍵盤焦點不正確地移到而不顯示參與者清單的聊天歷程記錄。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ffe95-960">Fix an issue where, when using the keyboard to view the list of participants in an IM conversion, the keyboard focus incorrectly moves to chat history instead of showing the list of participants.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="ffe95-961">修正問題時使用高對比 Windows 佈景主題的參與者動作畫面工具提示會消失。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ffe95-961">Fix an issue where the tooltips on the Participant Actions screen disappear when using a high contrast Windows theme.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="ffe95-962">修正問題不會議邀請中所示的電話號碼的位置。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ffe95-962">Fix an issue where the location of phone numbers isn't shown in meeting invites.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="ffe95-963">用滑鼠指標在具有高 DPI 遠端控制案例中修正的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ffe95-963">Fix an issue with the mouse pointer in remote control scenarios with high DPI.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="ffe95-964">參與者無法看到所顯示的其他參與者切換的共用的桌面時的共用的桌面修正問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ffe95-964">Fix an issue where a participant can't see the shared desktop when other participants switch which shared desktop is being displayed.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="ffe95-965">修正問題登入失敗時使用的憑證問題的位置。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ffe95-965">Fix an issue where sign in fails with a certificate issue.</span></span>

-   <span data-ttu-id="ffe95-970">修正簽發者其中重新加入會議設定內部 proxy pac 檔案中的 Url 為自動設定指令碼的 Internet Explorer 的電腦上會失敗。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ffe95-970">Fix an issuer where rejoining a meeting fails on computers configured for internal proxy pac file URLs in Internet Explorer as an automatic configuration script.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="ffe95-971">修正的問題時使用快速鍵設為靜音或關閉程序的影片，螢幕助讀程式，例如 [朗讀程式]，不要聲明所做的變更。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ffe95-971">Fix an issue where, when using keyboard shortcuts to mute or turn off a video, screen readers, such as Narrator, don't announce the changes.</span></span>

-   <span data-ttu-id="ffe95-973">修正問題其中螢幕助讀程式，例如 [朗讀程式]、 不正確地處理功能區底下只會顯示提醒通知。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ffe95-973">Fix an issue where screen readers, such as Narrator, don't correctly handle the alert notifications that appear just under the ribbon.</span></span>

### <a name="word-non-security-updates"></a><span data-ttu-id="ffe95-1008">Word： 的非安全性更新</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ffe95-1008">Word: Non-security updates</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="ffe95-1009">修正問題時執行另存新檔的資料夾含有大量的檔案，例如超過 30000 檔案 Word 損毀。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ffe95-1009">Fix an issue where Word crashes when doing a Save As to a folder that contains a large number of files, such as over 30,000 files.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="ffe95-1010">修正的問題時使用 InsertXML 方法，中斷的圖片連結的版面配置區顯示的位置，而不是實際的圖像。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ffe95-1010">Fix an issue where, when using the InsertXML method, a placeholder for a broken picture link is shown instead of the actual image.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="ffe95-1011">修正問題其中 Word 在執行另存新檔時，使用者已經選取當連接關閉時的 Office 文件快取中刪除檔案選項。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ffe95-1011">Fix an issue where Word crashes when doing a Save As and the user has selected the option to delete files from the Office Document Cache when they are closed.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="ffe95-1012">修正問題時執行另存新檔的資料夾含有大量的檔案，例如超過 30000 檔案 Word 損毀。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ffe95-1012">Fix an issue where Word crashes when doing a Save As to a folder that contains a large number of files, such as over 30,000 files.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="ffe95-1013">修正問題 CTRL + ALT + 4 捷徑不輸入位置歐元符號時使用英國鍵盤。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ffe95-1013">Fix an issue where the CTRL+ALT+4 shortcut doesn't type the Euro sign when using a UK keyboard.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="ffe95-1014">修正問題其中焦點會切換至小型] 對話方塊中的右上角，輸入東亞文字分隔字元使用輸入法 (IME) 時，且使用者無法再繼續編輯文件。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ffe95-1014">Fix an issue where the focus switches to a small dialog box in the upper right corner when typing East Asian characters using an Input Method Editor (IME) and then the user can't continue editing the document.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="ffe95-1015">修正問題其中字型變更為 Segoe UI Emoji 時使用日文輸入的法 (IME) 時輸入雙位元組字元設 (DBCS) 符號字元。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ffe95-1015">Fix an issue where the font is changed to Segoe UI Emoji when inputting double-byte character set (DBCS) symbol characters when using the Japanese input method editor (IME).</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="ffe95-1016">修正問題不正確地提供部落認證嘗試發佈至 SharePoint 部落格文章時提示使用者。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ffe95-1016">Fix an issue where the user is incorrectly prompted to provide Blogger credentials when trying to publish a blog post to SharePoint.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="ffe95-1017">修正問題的使用者變更預設編輯或校訂語言，不會變更延續至下一次開啟 Word 時。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ffe95-1017">Fix an issue that when the user changes the default editing or proofing language, that change doesn't carry over to the next time Word is opened.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="ffe95-1018">修正問題其中開啟需要表單型驗證的伺服器上的文件會導致 Word 損毀。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ffe95-1018">Fix an issue where opening a document on a server that requires forms-based authentication causes Word to crash.</span></span>

### <a name="office-suite-feature-updates"></a><span data-ttu-id="ffe95-1019">Office 套件： 更新的功能</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ffe95-1019">Office suite: Feature updates</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="ffe95-1020">**授權的 token 更新共用電腦啟用：** Office 會嘗試更新共用的電腦啟用規則為基礎的授權權杖之後權杖到期 50%，以協助使用者不一定要能存取網際網路。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ffe95-1020">**Licensing token renewal for shared computer activation:** Office attempts to renew the licensing token for shared computer activation on a regular basis once the token is 50% expired, to help users who don't always have Internet access.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="ffe95-1021">**共用的電腦啟用降低功能的模式：** 當使用共用的電腦啟用，如果使用者關閉 [登入] 視窗或使用者授權憑證過期，使用者仍然可以使用的 Office 應用程式但應用程式將處於精簡的功能模式。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ffe95-1021">**Reduced functionality mode for shared computer activation:** When using shared computer activation, if the user closes the sign-in window or the user's licensing token expires, the user can still use the Office app, but the app will be in reduced functionality mode.</span></span>

### <a name="office-suite-non-security-updates"></a><span data-ttu-id="ffe95-1027">Office 套件： 的非安全性更新</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ffe95-1027">Office suite: Non-security updates</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="ffe95-1028">修正問題的可能會造成停止運作或不正確地顯示 frames 疊置順序的 VBA 表單。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ffe95-1028">Fix an issue with VBA forms that can cause the z-order of frames to stop functioning or display incorrectly.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="ffe95-1029">修正問題其中 trigged System Center Configuration Manager 更新 UpdateChannel 設定變更登錄中為某個項目不是有效的更新通道。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ffe95-1029">Fix an issue where an update trigged by System Center Configuration Manager changes the UpdateChannel setting in the registry to something that's not a valid update channel.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="ffe95-1030">其中時的 OneDrive for Business 網站並使用 OneDrive sync 用戶端的本機電腦將檔案同步處理，, 從 URL 開啟同步處理後檔案儲存會使 Word、 Excel、 或 PowerPoint hang 修正問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ffe95-1030">Fix an issue where, when files are synced from a OneDrive for Business site to a local computer using the OneDrive sync client, saving a synced back file that was opened from a URL causes Word, Excel, or PowerPoint to hang.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="ffe95-1031">具有 VBA 表單控制項有會導致透明 label 控制項看起來不透明、 可能會造成不會再出現或運作如預期般運作，現有的表單和會導致 Office 應用程式停止回應時嘗試開啟啟用巨集檔案的修正問題包含表單控制項。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ffe95-1031">Fix an issue with VBA form controls that can cause transparent label controls to appear opaque, can cause existing forms to no longer appear or work as expected, and can cause the Office application to stop responding when attempting to open a macro-enabled file that contains form controls.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="ffe95-1032">修正的問題時使用的受管理的中繼資料屬性，[顯示詳細資料] 按鈕會出現在 [屬性] 區段中 [檔案\>而不是所設定的中繼資料值的資訊。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ffe95-1032">Fix an issue where, when using managed metadata properties, a "Show Details" button appears in the Properties section under File \> Info instead of the metadata values that are set.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="ffe95-1033">修正問題 [說明] 窗格內顯示的位置與不同資料庫] 對話方塊中，而不是將應用程式時使用直接命令 me.時選取 [取得說明</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ffe95-1033">Fix an issue where the Help pane appears as a separate dialog box, instead of within the application, when selecting Get Help when using Tell Me.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="ffe95-1034">修正問題 OfficeC2RClient.exe 其中不能 「 通道 」 辨識為選用設定。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ffe95-1034">Fix an issue where OfficeC2RClient.exe doesn't recognize "channel" as an optional setting.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="ffe95-1035">修正問題出新的版本及組建格式不會顯示在 Office 更新區段的 [檔案\>帳戶。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ffe95-1035">Fix an issue where the new version and build format doesn't show in the Office Updates section under File \> Account.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="ffe95-1036">其中切換到不同的更新通道可能會導致安裝下一次更新程序會執行舊版組建修正問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ffe95-1036">Fix an issue where switching to a different update channel may result in an earlier build being installed the next time the update process is run.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="ffe95-1037">搭配使用 GDI 印表機驅動程式 V3 版本的印表機列印修正問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ffe95-1037">Fix an issue with printing to printers that use a V3 version of the GDI printer driver.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="ffe95-1038">修正問題時執行線上修復安裝使用者介面 (UI) 不會出現的位置。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ffe95-1038">Fix an issue where the installation user interface (UI) doesn't appear when performing an Online Repair.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="ffe95-1039">其中 「 線上範本的搜尋 」 方塊仍啟用即使在存取線上範本已停用的群組原則設定或登錄設定後修正問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ffe95-1039">Fix an issue where the "Search for online templates" box is still enabled even after access to online templates has been disabled by a Group Policy setting or a registry setting.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="ffe95-1040">其中，開啟 Office 應用程式、 時，使用者會收到錯誤訊息 Microsoft 找不到授權的應用程式及修復嘗試已失敗或取消，然後按一下 [Office 應用程式的問題會關閉的修正程式。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ffe95-1040">Fix an issue where, when opening an Office app, the user receives an error message that Microsoft can't find the license for the application and that a repair attempt was unsuccessful or cancelled, and then the Office app closes.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="ffe95-1041">修正問題導致設為大於它們應該是先前建立的更新的下載項目大小的二進位差異壓縮。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ffe95-1041">Fix an issue with binary delta compression causing the size of the downloads for the updates for the previous build to be larger than they should be.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="ffe95-1042">修正問題 Office 更新任務太常執行的位置，而造成增加 CPU 使用量和桌面圖示簡要閃爍或重新整理。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ffe95-1042">Fix an issue where the Office Update task runs too frequently, causing increased CPU usage and desktop icons to briefly flash or refresh.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="ffe95-1043">修正問題其中執行 Office 位於相同的多個使用者的時間在單一電腦上具有特定權限設定原因損毀的 Office 應用程式。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ffe95-1043">Fix an issue where multiple users running Office at the same time on a single computer with a specific permissions configuration causes Office apps to crash.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="ffe95-1044">修正問題其中使用 Office 增益集的命令會使 Excel、 Word 或 PowerPoint 隨機損毀。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ffe95-1044">Fix an issue where using Office add-in commands causes Excel, Word, or PowerPoint to randomly crash.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="ffe95-1045">修正其中更新 Office ODBC 登錄項目會覆寫及需要 Microsoft Access 資料庫引擎可轉散發套件重新安裝或修復問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ffe95-1045">Fix an issue where updating Office overwrites ODBC registry entries and requires the Microsoft Access Database Engine Redistributable to be reinstalled or repaired.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="ffe95-1046">修正問題其中 PowerPoint、 Word 或 Excel 在從 URL，例如存新檔 SharePoint、 開啟 Office 文件及 URL 結尾時 / 字元。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="ffe95-1046">Fix an issue where PowerPoint, Word, or Excel crashes when an Office document is opened from a URL, such as from SharePoint, and the URL ends with the / character.</span></span>
